<P>jay1atu lokezwara nAtha abhay1e bAluMkA

<P>saMsAra nAzAMgatA tuhi se siddha y1ekA | 1 |

<P>zuddha saSTika nirAkuLa nirastaka

<P>nizAkara mauLi nAtha jay1atu triy1ambaka | 2 |

<P>agAda saMsAra sAgara aTai y1e mAy1A

<P>samasta goSThI kalu nAtha hoi y1eka kAy1A | 3 |

<P>bhogeNa bhoga swAmI rogeNa pramAda

<P>samasta upekSi cintilu paramapada | 4 |

<P>nirAkAra puruSa nikaLaMka kAy1AgoTi

<P>anIti saMsAru mote uddhara dhrujaTI | 5 |

<P1>2| zuddha saSTika nirAkuLa nILakaNu nikaLaMka candra
<>nizAkara mauLi deba jay1atu kAzIrudra | (Ta)

<P1>4|1 bhogeNa bhogI swAmI bhAbeNa apramAda | (adhikAMza pothi)

[MBO-08-2]

<P>kAmyeka puruSa nAtha kAminI arddhakAy1A

<P>kAma nizodhana nAtha aboGgtra saday1A | 6 |

<P>nay1ana pan~chadaza swabhAbe kuNDaLI

<P>girijAra saGge ye sAmaratha trizULI | 7 |

<P>sajjana janara tu hrudagate japAmALi

<P>bhairoba mUrati dhari chApilu mahAbaLI | 8 |

<P>zireNa dhabaLI ye pinAkI dhanurddhara | 9 |

<P>andheka binAzilu bALalILA beLe | 10 |

<P>yogeNa yogezwara swAmI samare jagujitA

<P>namo namo deba nILakaNTha nirAlamba zwetarUpI

<P>muhiM talay1e karai dibArAtre heTi | 14 |

<P>yoge yogezwara swAmI gyAna upagata

[MBO-08-3]

<P>saindu bAma ghora tatapurukha IzAna

<P>nandI mahAkALa tule kApALI bidyamAna | 18 |

<P>somapALa mantre say1aLa jana tArantA

<P>iha paralokakaiM pALana karantA | 19 |

<P>jay1atu jagabandhu prabhma digAmbara

<P>y1e bhaba bArAdhi madhyuM bAreka uddhara | 20 |

<P>catrabhUa dekhiNa se mAnagobinda
